         </a>
         <p itemprop="headline" class="hgpm-image-hed js-asset-headline placeholder-bg external-link">
          Everything you need to know about the American Music Awards
         </p>
         <span class="hgpm-list-wrap js-list-wrap">
          <span class="hgpm-list-image-wrap">
           <img src="" itemprop="thumbnailUrl" class="hgpm-list-image js-asset-image" data-src="http://www.gannett-cdn.com/-mm-/da62e4e52e0ce1a8b96e18d79f4dc4caad965165/c=3-0-1596-900&amp;r=x83&amp;c=140x80/local/-/media/2016/11/20/PAGroup/FlipSidePA/636152270057717873-636150893940033997-drake.png" width="140" height="80" data-crop="16_9" />
           <span class="hgpm-image-text-hed-icon js-asset-disposable">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="hgpm-list-text ">
           <span itemprop="headline" class="hgpm-list-hed js-asset-headline placeholder-bg external-link">
            Everything you need to know about the American Music Awards
           </span>
           <span class="hgpm-back-listview-text js-asset-description placeholder-bg" data-fulltext="Unlike the Grammys, where an academy of music industry professionals decides who receives awards, the American Music Awards are entirely fan-voted, putting the power in the listeners' hands.">
            Unlike the Grammys, where an academy of music industry professionals decides who receives awards, the American Music Awards are entirely fan-voted, putting the power in the listeners&#39; hands.
           </span>

        mainAd.style.cssText = 'height:1px; width:1px; overflow:auto;position: absolute;left: -999em;';
        document.body.appendChild(mainAd);
        var blockPosition = document.getElementById('main_ad');
        if(blockPosition &amp;&amp; blockPosition.offsetHeight == 1) {
            window.adsEnabled = true;
        }
  </script>
 </body>
</html>
